<Text>UPDATE:  the quote Google has chosen is NOT in reference to this facility, but another by the same company. Please read full review! Google, please correct.

This place could be fantastic. COULD. I genuinely like this gym, but its sorely lacking in TLC and effective management.

I give it three stars because they have a pool and awesome amenities like hot tub, cold plunge, sauna, and steam room.

However, they are sorely lacking in maintenance, cleanliness, and overall some very basic things (soap in the bathroom anyone?). If something breaks, don't expect it to be fixed. There's a water fountain in the women's locker room that has been broken and non-functional for well over a month. The door to the sauna is made out of glass and metal (yeah, METAL in a sauna) and the handle has been hastily taped over with foam insulation to keep you from burning yourself. The towels are dingy and old (if you can find any). Clogged drains, broken shower heads, missing hooks and shower curtains, broken mirrors in the workout areas... the list goes on.

Ironically, the brand new club on Meridian is top notch! They have the latest and greatest equipment and sparkling facilities. No pool and spa style locker rooms though.

It's clear that Fitness Evolution's corporate offices has dedicated all their resources to this new facility. But when you leave your "Elite" location in such disarray, that's simply poor business practices. All we want is for things to actually work and be clean. That's not asking for much.

You are only as strong as your weakest link.</Text><pics>None< /pics>< resp>

<time>1485039511397<//time>< Text>
This is the abandoned step-child of the Fitness Evolution chain. It it The most poorly maintained, dirty, sad fitness club I've ever been to. They've cancelled all of the group exercise classes and yet they call this location an "elite" facility.  Junk is piled up everywhere for months, no one maintains any of the rooms, the two custodial staff per day are only there for limited hours and can't come close to keeping up. 100% of the deck chairs at the pool are broken and have been for almost a year. The only positives here are the location, the steam, the pool, the nice clientele -- and the fact that there is actually a lot of good equipment and space to work out if you can put up with the crappy facility.  If all you want is to get in, work out and get out -- you'll be ok. If you want amenities, forget it. Some of the staff try their best, but FitEvo corporation gives them nothing to work with.  The employees are like sailors on a sinking ship. The positive reviews for this location are bogus, definitely posted by employees.< /Text>

< text>
Great gym, wonderful trainers. What really makes this place so awesome is the fact that the trainers are so knowledgeable. I was very impressed. This particular facility also has a heated swimming pool all year round. There's steam rooms and there is even a small workout area in the women's locker room. Thats actually nice for women who get together to workout and don't want to do all their cardio out on the main floor. There are small seats for seniors in the women's shower room - which is nice for people who are older or even the disabled. There are big light up mirrors and even television sets in the women's locker room. As I mentioned the trainers are super knowledgable. Knowledgeable and friendly. That is a win-win.<//text>

<Review>Member since 27 November AD-2015

[86 days]

Located adjacent to the First Unitarian Church of San Jose, and across the street from Saint James Park, is the Masonic Lodge built in the 1924th year of our Lord. As of the time which this synopsis was written the building is owned by Mr. Barry Swenson, who counts Gold's Gym as a lessee: Fitness Evolution is a subsidiary of that corporation.

The cost is approximately $43/month, which is drastically less than could be expected considering the potential clientele. Potential downsides are that the organization is not in control of the lease (assumption), there is riffraff which brings a low-class element, and as has been mentioned in previous reviews there are some things that are to be desired, although during February 2016 there are renovations to the locker-rooms which suggest a gradual update is being implemented or phased in.

The other gymnasium which bears the same name in the immediate vicinity is significantly smaller and without the novel amenities which are particular to this location. Said features include the Pool (consisting of 5 lanes), the Sauna & Steam Room (a set of 2), a Massage room, plenty of space for relaxing poolside (e.g., outdoor space which is fenced off with a high wall), and the basketball court which is part of the eastern section of the facility (an add-on from the original temple complex).

The staff does not espouse animosity or duplicity, and is consistently professional. Although relatively young (taken as a mean), the haughty air that had plagued the previous establishment is absent: they are courteous and make an effort to welcome persons with more than a modicum of sincerity.</Review>< rating>
3< /rating>

< text>
TL;DR: They're slow af and the manager will try to rip you off if you look like you don't know cars. AKA me, a young asian chick. Go somewhere else or have someone who knows cars go with you.

Back in May this year, I went in to get a flat tire checked and replaced if necessary. I got in at 11am and they said they'll "definitely be done by the time they close."
So I come back at 5:30 because they close at 6. It wasn't done yet, so I didn't mind waiting a while. At 5:55, I see my tire hasn't moved at all. I ask about it, and THEN they start working on it. The technician is attentive and patient, but the manager says to him, "This is on you. I'm leaving exactly at 6, I have a wife to get to and a dinner to eat," which is a terrible way to treat your staff.

< Text>
This is one of the better GW stores imo. The donation receiving area is around the side of building rather than behind, making it easier to drop off donations.  Parking is not a problem as it's in a plaza sharing ample space with nearby businesses. Staff are always friendly and available for helping customers. For instance, an older woman had fallen on her way out and she was instantly helped to her feet by a quick witted staff member. And on a personal note, this store doesn't seem to smell as musty as many other thrift stores, if that's not your thing.< /Text>

<Text>Experience:
With the pandemic in full effect, I spent a year doing virtual window shopping for cars since I had the luxury of working from home.
I initially found my 2019 Ford fusion online. I reached out to see if I could get a test drive and got connected with their internet sales consultant, David Padilla. That morning was pretty smooth. I showed up and the car was right by the driveway ready to go for the test drive -- definitely schedule an appointment a few days ahead of time.

The test drive was solo. I took my time feeling the car out. I am 6'1 and have a football player build. With that being said, It was very easy to slip in and out of the car. When I got back, the process was like an assembly line, very smooth and no real hold-ups. When everything was ready to go,  David offered to deliver my car to my home since I came to the dealership solo. He was super helpful and attentive. Total process took about 3 hours from I arrived to when I got home with the new car.

Financing:
Based off of my credit Report and what my options were, I told them I did not want to pay over a certain amount with the added features and services. They were more than accommodating and I did not feel any remorse over my purchase.

Overall:
It has been about a month and I am very happy with my car. I remember telling Mr. Padilla, " I'm aiming for the path of least resistance" meaning I didn't want to overcomplicate things. Not sure if that meant much, but my experience was very smooth. If I was ever in the need for a pick up or an  SUV, I'd definitely come back.

Pros :
No pandering.
Process was smooth.
Home Delivery was super helpful.

Cons:
Physical location - dealership is on both sides of the main road  in town. Even though my car was "Used" car, it was in the "New" car side of the dealership. Not a big deal except the road was a 4 lane Boulevard  and the crossing intersections were not close by.

I'd still recommend these awesome people 5 stars!< /Text><Pictures>None</Pictures><Resp>None<//Resp>< gmapID>

- unbalanced front tires (on day 1 after driving it off the yard),
- bad battery (within the 1st month), and
- Leaky axle seal on both rear wheels with the fluid contaminating the brake pads and rotors. (at about 1 month)

Alright, one faulty item is not a big deal, but 3 issues (excl. the brake  pads and rotors) within a couple of months is stretching my believe that the inspection was thorough. (let's call it 3 stars - it's ok to have an off day).

< review>
My wife and I live 1,300 miles away from this dealer. We do not buy cars often (4 cars in 20 years). After searching for a used 2017 Mustang convertible nationwide (assisted by USAA online car buying service), we engaged Bill Brandt Ford because the car we wanted was available from them at a great price.

During our pre-sale engagement, our salesman was Corey. He was patient, courteous, responsive and attentive to our every inquiry along the way. As we progressed in the pre-sales, he even acted upon our request for a remote, front-to-back tour of the vehicle via FaceTime so that we could see the car without being there in-person. He really seems to like his work and he is really good at it.

We flew 1,400 miles to Sacramento and then drove the hour to Brentwood to purchase our vehicle at 9AM on a Saturday morning. When we arrived and looked at the car, we found it to be just as it was represented over FaceTime, via CarFax, and via our conversations with the dealer. Corey was true, forthright, and trustworthy in his dealings with us.

We enjoyed the entire pre-sales and signing experience. The closing paperwork was completed quickly (it took only about 15 minutes after waiting for about 30 minutes for the documentation to be prepared) and was a pleasant experience.

We learned during closing that Bill Brandt Ford is a family-owned (not corporate-owned) dealership unlike a majority of Ford dealerships in California. The difference is palpable.

We are delighted with our purchase. We drove home (two-day drive) in our new vehicle, with no regrets and no buyer's remorse...fully delighted. Enjoying our Mustang!

We would definitely recommend Bill Brandt Ford to anyone, wherever they live, based upon our great buying experience. No regrets.<//review>
